# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repositories (version-pinned mirrors):**

- `github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0$` filter
- `github.com/sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0$` filter
- `github.com/sg-evals/api--v0.32.0` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/api--v0.32.0$` filter
- `github.com/sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd$` filter

Scope ALL keyword_search/nls_search queries to these repos.
Use the repo name as the `repo` parameter for read_file/go_to_definition/find_references.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kubernetes ConfigMap Immutability Feature Migration

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in kubernetes/kubernetes that implement the ConfigMap and Secret immutability feature: the Immutable field validation, the mutation prevention logic, and the watch optimization that skips immutable objects.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the migration domain.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd` (etcd-io/etcd)

66-assistanttext-
Perfect! I've successfully identified and documented all the Go source files that implement the ConfigMap and Secret immutability feature in Kubernetes v1.32.0. Here's a summary of what I found:

## ConfigMap and Secret Immutability Feature Implementation

The immutability feature is implemented across these key areas:

### **1. Type Definitions**
- **pkg/apis/core/types.go**: Internal type definitions for Secret and ConfigMap with Immutable field
- **staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/types.go**: Public API type definitions with Immutable field

### **2. Field Validation**
- **pkg/apis/core/validation/validation.go**: Contains:
  - `ValidateSecretUpdate()` - Validates immutable Secret constraints
  - `ValidateConfigMapUpdate()` - Validates immutable ConfigMap constraints  
  - `ValidateImmutableField()` - Helper for immutability validation

### **3. REST API Strategy Layer**
- **pkg/registry/core/secret/strategy.go**: Strategy implementation calling ValidateSecretUpdate
- **pkg/registry/core/configmap/strategy.go**: Strategy implementation calling ValidateConfigMapUpdate

### **4. Watch Optimization (the key feature)**
- **pkg/kubelet/util/manager/watch_based_manager.go**: Core watch-based manager that:
  - Defines `isImmutableFunc` type for checking immutability
  - In `objectCache.Get()`, detects immutable objects and stops their watches
  - Maintains `objectCacheItem.immutable` flag to prevent reflector restart

### **5. Manager Implementations**
- **pkg/kubelet/secret/secret_manager.go**: NewWatchingSecretManager creates isImmutable callback
- **pkg/kubelet/configmap/configmap_manager.go**: NewWatchingConfigMapManager creates isImmutable callback

### **6. Tests**
- **pkg/apis/core/validation/validation_test.go**: Comprehensive test coverage for immutability validation

\tmaxIdleTime time.Duration,\n184: \tstopCh <-chan struct{}) Store {\n185: \n186: \tif maxIdleTime < minIdleTime {\n187: \t\tmaxIdleTime = minIdleTime\n188: \t}\n189: \n190: \tstore := &objectCache{\n191: \t\tlistObject:    listObject,\n192: \t\twatchObject:   watchObject,\n193: \t\tnewObject:     newObject,\n194: \t\tisImmutable:   isImmutable,\n195: \t\tgroupResource: wait.Until(store.startRecycleIdleWatch, time.Minute, stopCh)\n202: \tgo store.shutdownWhenStopped(stopCh)\n203: \treturn store\n204: }\n205: \n206: func (c *objectCache) newStore() *cacheStore {\n207: \t// TODO: We may consider created a dedicated store keeping just a single\n208: \t// item, instead of using a generic store implementation for this purpose.\n209: \t// However, simple benchmarks show that memory overhead in that case is\n210: \t// decrease from ~600B to ~300B per object. So we are not optimizing it\n211: \t// until we will see a good reason for that.\n212: \tstore := cache.NewStore(cache.MetaNamespaceKeyFunc)\n213: \treturn &cacheStore{store, sync.Mutex{}, false}\n214: }\n215: \n216: func (c *objectCache) newReflectorLocked(namespace, name string) *objectCacheItem {\n217: \tfieldSelector := fields.Set{\"metadata.name\": name}.AsSelector().String()\n218: \tlistFunc := func(options metav1.ListOptions) (runtime.Object, error) {\n219: \t\toptions.FieldSelector = fieldSelector\n220: \t\treturn c.listObject(namespace, options)\n221: \t}\n222: \twatchFunc := func(options metav1.ListOptions) (watch.Interface, error) {\n223: \t\toptions.FieldSelector = fieldSelector\n224: \t\treturn c.watchObject(namespace, options)\n225: \t}\n226: \tstore := \t\tcache.ReflectorOptions{\n232: \t\t\tName: fmt.Sprintf(\"object-%q/%q\", namespace, name),\n233: \t\t\t// Bump default 5m MinWatchTimeout to avoid recreating\n234: \t\t\t// watches too often.\n235: \t\t\tMinWatchTimeout: 30 * time.Minute,\n236: \t\t},\n237: \t)\n238: \titem := &objectCacheItem{\n239: \t\trefMap:    make(map[types.UID]int),\n240: \t\tstore:     store,\n241: \t\treflector: reflector,\n242: \t\thasSynced: func() (bool, error) { return store.hasSynced(), nil },\n243: \t\tstopCh:    make(chan struct{}),\n244: \t}\n245: \n246: \t// Don't start reflector if Kubelet is already shutting down.\n247: \tif !c.stopped {\n248: \t\tgo item.startReflector()\n249: \t}\n250: \treturn item\n251: }\n252: \n253: func (c *objectCache) AddReference(namespace, name string, referencedFrom types.UID) {\n254: \tkey := objectKey{namespace: namespace, name: name}\n255: \n256: \t// AddReference is called from RegisterPod thus it needs to be efficient.\n257: \t// Thus, it is only increasing refCount and in case of first registration\n258: \t// of a given object it starts corresponding reflector.\n259: \t// It's responsibility of the first Get operation to wait until the\n260: \t// reflector propagated the store.\n261: \tc.lock.Lock()\n262: \tdefer c.lock.Unlock()\n263: \titem, exists := c.items[key]\n264: \tif !exists {\n265: \t\titem = referencedFrom types.UID) {\n272: \tkey := objectKey{namespace: namespace, name: name}\n273: \n274: \tc.lock.Lock()\n275: \tdefer c.lock.Unlock()\n276: \tif item, ok := c.items[key]; ok {\n277: \t\titem.refMap[referencedFrom]--\n278: \t\tif item.refMap[referencedFrom] == 0 {\n279: \t\t\tdelete(item.refMap, referencedFrom)\n280: \t\t}\n281: \t\tif len(item.refMap) == 0 {\n282: \t\t\t// Stop the underlying reflector.\n283: \t\t\titem.stop()\n284: \t\t\tdelete(c.items, key)\n285: \t\t}\n286: \t}\n287: }\n288: \n289: // key returns key of an object with a given name and namespace.\n290: // This has to be in-sync with cache.MetaNamespaceKeyFunc.\n291: func (c *objectCache) key(namespace, name string) string {\n292: \tif len(namespace) > 0 {\n293: \t\treturn namespace + \"/\" + name\n294: \t}\n295: \treturn name\n296: }\n297: \n298: func (c *objectCache) isStopped() bool {\n299: \tc.lock.RLock()\n300: \tdefer c.lock.RUnlock()\n301: \treturn c.stopped\n302: }\n303: \n304: func (c *objectCache) Get(namespace, name string) (runtime.Object, error) {\n305: \tkey := objectKey{namespace: namespace, name: name}\n306: \n307: \tc.lock.RLock()\n308: \titem, exists := c.items[key]\n309: \tc.lock.RUnlock()\n310: \n311: \tif !exists {\n312: \t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"object %q/%q not registered\", namespace, name)\n313: \t}\n314: \t// Record last access time independently if it \t\t// If the returned object is immutable, stop the reflector.\n334: \t\t//\n335: \t\t// NOTE: we may potentially not even start the reflector if the object is\n336: \t\t// already immutable.
